#RUOTSI     ---
#ENGL       
#OHJE_S  
Includes: Laparotomy, thoracolaparotomy, laparoscopy
Includes: Freeing of adhesions for access or exploration
Operations for adhesions causing obstruction, see: JFK
Gynecolocical operations for adhesions, see: LBF
Biopsy of peritoneum, see: JAL
Drainage and irrigation, see: JAJ, JAK
Percutaneous puncture, ascites tap, irrigation of peritoneal cavity and peritoneal dialysis, see: TJA
In operations that can only be performed by laparotomy, a separate code for the laparotomy should not be used

#RUOTSI     ---
#ENGL       Anus and perianal tissue
#OHJE_S  
Because transluminal endoscopic operations on the anal canal are identical with open operations with or without the use of e.g. a bivalve retractor, transluminal endoscopic procedures are not definedAnoscopy, see: UJH 02
#OHJE_R

#KOODI_A    JJC
#MUUT_PVM   1995/10/12
#KAYTPVM    1996/01/01
#POISTPVM       /  /  
#SUOMI      Transplantation of liver and related operations
#RUOTSI     ---
#ENGL       
#OHJE_S  
Procedures on liver, biliary passages or hepatic vessels after previous transplantation that are identical to procedures on the innate liver are classified as such
Biopsy, exploration, see: TJJ or JJA
Resection of previously transplanted liver, see: JJB
Reconstruction of biliary passages, see: JKD
Vascular reconstructions, see: Chapter P
Donor hepatectomy, see: YJJ
#OHJE_R

#SUOMI      Transplantation of pancreas and related operations
#RUOTSI     ---
#ENGL       
#OHJE_S  
Allogenic transplantations are from cadaver donor unless otherwise specified
Procedures on previously transplantated pancreas that are identical to procedures on the innate pancreas are classified as such
Biopsy, exploration, see:TJL or JLA
Partial excision of previously transplanted pancreas, see: JLC
Donor pancreatectomy, see: YJL

#KOODI_R    JW

#POISTPVM       /  /  
#SUOMI      Reoperations in gastroenterological surgery
#RUOTSI     ---
#ENGL       Reoperations in gastroenterological surgery
#OHJE_S  
Puncture, needle biopsy and other minor procedures, see: TC
Digits 0, 3 and 6:
Note: Procedures not otherwise specified in the code texts are open operations or procedures
Digits 1, 4 and 7:
Includes (Chapter J): Laparoscopy, laparoscopic and thoracoscopic procedures
Includes: Use of auxiliary stabs or minor incisions. The procedure is classified as laparoscopic or thoracoscopic if dissection and preparation of the organ in question is performed endoscopically, ev
Note: In the code texts, these procedures are specified as thoracoscopic or laparoscopic
Digits 2, 5 and 8:
Includes (Chapter J): Procedures in the course of oesophagoscopy, gastroscopy, enteroscopy, coloscopy, sigmoidoscopy
Note: The term "endoscopic" in code texts implies transluminal endoscopic procedures
For codes with the fourth posision digit 9 (the"other" codes), only the last digits 6, 7 and 8 are used, with significance as above.
Please note the following difference between transluminal endoscopy and invasive or therapeutic procedures performed in the course of transluminal endoscopy:
Transluminal endoscopy, frequently allowing examination of several connected organ cavities, is generally classified (in Chapter U) according to the most common main target for the category of endosco
Endoscopic procedures are classified according to the location where they are actually performed, and then by action and technique.
In Chapter J, e.g.transluminal endoscopic polypectomy in small intestine may be performed at gastroscopy, enteroscopy, coloscopy or ERCP
Includes: Surgery of digestive system and spleen
#OHJE_R
